\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00575}00575\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ defines\ an\ action\ that\ can\ be\ used\ in\ a\ mock\ function.\ \ Typically,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00576}00576\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ these\ actions\ only\ care\ about\ a\ subset\ of\ the\ arguments\ of\ the\ mock}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00577}00577\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ function.\ \ For\ example,\ if\ such\ an\ action\ only\ uses\ the\ second}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00578}00578\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ argument,\ it\ can\ be\ used\ in\ any\ mock\ function\ that\ takes\ >=\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00579}00579\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arguments\ where\ the\ type\ of\ the\ second\ argument\ is\ compatible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00580}00580\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00581}00581\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Therefore,\ the\ action\ implementation\ must\ be\ prepared\ to\ take\ more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00582}00582\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arguments\ than\ it\ needs.\ \ The\ ExcessiveArg\ type\ is\ used\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00583}00583\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ represent\ those\ excessive\ arguments.\ \ In\ order\ to\ keep\ the\ compiler}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00584}00584\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ error\ messages\ tractable,\ we\ define\ it\ in\ the\ testing\ namespace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00585}00585\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ instead\ of\ testing::internal.\ \ However,\ this\ is\ an\ INTERNAL\ TYPE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00586}00586\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ subject\ to\ change\ without\ notice,\ so\ a\ user\ MUST\ NOT\ USE\ THIS}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00864}00864\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ ACTION*\ family\ of\ macros\ can\ be\ used\ in\ a\ namespace\ scope\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00865}00865\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ define\ custom\ actions\ easily.\ \ The\ syntax:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00866}00866\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00867}00867\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ ACTION(name)\ \{\ statements;\ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00868}00868\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00869}00869\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ define\ an\ action\ with\ the\ given\ name\ that\ executes\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00870}00870\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ statements.\ \ The\ value\ returned\ by\ the\ statements\ will\ be\ used\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00871}00871\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ return\ value\ of\ the\ action.\ \ Inside\ the\ statements,\ you\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00872}00872\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ refer\ to\ the\ K-\/th\ (0-\/based)\ argument\ of\ the\ mock\ function\ by}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00875}00875\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ ACTION(IncrementArg1)\ \{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00878}00878\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00879}00879\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00880}00880\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ allows\ you\ to\ write}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00884}00884\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ You\ can\ also\ refer\ to\ the\ entire\ argument\ tuple\ and\ its\ type\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00885}00885\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 'args'\ and\ 'args\_type',\ and\ refer\ to\ the\ mock\ function\ type\ and\ its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00886}00886\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ return\ type\ by\ 'function\_type'\ and\ 'return\_type'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00887}00887\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00888}00888\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ you\ don't\ need\ to\ specify\ the\ types\ of\ the\ mock\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00889}00889\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arguments.\ \ However\ rest\ assured\ that\ your\ code\ is\ still\ type-\/safe:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00890}00890\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ you'll\ get\ a\ compiler\ error\ if\ *arg1\ doesn't\ support\ the\ ++}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00891}00891\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operator,\ or\ if\ the\ type\ of\ ++(*arg1)\ isn't\ compatible\ with\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00892}00892\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ mock\ function's\ return\ type,\ for\ example.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00893}00893\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00937}00937\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ While\ it's\ tempting\ to\ always\ use\ the\ ACTION*\ macros\ when\ defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00938}00938\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ new\ action,\ you\ should\ also\ consider\ implementing\ ActionInterface}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00940}00940\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ use\ the\ action\ a\ lot.\ \ While\ these\ approaches\ require\ more\ work,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00941}00941\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ they\ give\ you\ more\ control\ on\ the\ types\ of\ the\ mock\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00942}00942\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arguments\ and\ the\ action\ parameters,\ which\ in\ general\ leads\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00943}00943\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ better\ compiler\ error\ messages\ that\ pay\ off\ in\ the\ long\ run.\ \ They}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00944}00944\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ also\ allow\ overloading\ actions\ based\ on\ parameter\ types\ (as\ opposed}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00946}00946\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00947}00947\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CAVEAT:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00949}00949\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ACTION*()\ can\ only\ be\ used\ in\ a\ namespace\ scope.\ \ The\ reason\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00950}00950\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ C++\ doesn't\ yet\ allow\ function-\/local\ types\ to\ be\ used\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00951}00951\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ instantiate\ templates.\ \ The\ up-\/coming\ C++0x\ standard\ will\ fix\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00952}00952\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Once\ that's\ done,\ we'll\ consider\ supporting\ using\ ACTION*()\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00953}00953\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ function.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00975}00975\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ cannot\ be\ inferred\ from\ its\ value\ parameters.\ \ ACTION()\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00976}00976\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ACTION\_P*()\ don't\ support\ that.\ \ ACTION\_TEMPLATE()\ remedies\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-actions_8h_source_l00977}00977\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ can\ be\ viewed\ as\ an\ extension\ to\ ACTION()\ and\ ACTION\_P*().}}
